classloading. The system is located in the 'sg-evals/kafka--0753c489' repository under the connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ package.\\n\\n## Core Architecture\\n\\n### ClassLoader Hierarchy\\nThe system uses a custom classloader hierarchy to provide plugin isolation:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that extends URLClassLoader and implements child-first delegation for loading isolated plugins. Each plugin location gets its own PluginClassLoader instance.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A URLClassLoader that delegates class loading to multiple PluginClassLoader instances based on the requested class. It maintains a registry of discovered plugins and routes class loading requests to the appropriate PluginClassLoader.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory class that creates both DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances with support for security manager compatibility.\\n\\n### Plugin Discovery Mechanism\\n\\nThe plugin scanning system uses reflection and Java ServiceLoader to discover plugins:\\n\\n1. **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java): Abstract base class defining the plugin scanning interface with methods to discover plugins from plugin sources.\\n\\n2. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Classgraph library to perform reflection-based discovery. It scans for concrete implementations of plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy) and collects version information via plugin reflection.\\n\\n3. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins registered in META-INF/services/ configuration files.\\n\\n4. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A Java record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, multi-JAR directory, or class hierarchy), including the ClassLoader and URLs to scan.\\n\\n### Plugin Metadata and Description\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc<T>** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): Generic descriptor class that holds metadata for a discovered plugin including the plugin class, version, type, and associated ClassLoader. Implements Comparable for sorting plugins by version and location.\\n\\n2. **PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java): Enumeration of plugin interface types: SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_POLICY.\\n\\n3. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Container for scan results holding sorted sets of PluginDesc instances for each plugin type, with support for merging multiple scan results.\\n\\n### Interface-Based Plugin Types\\n\\nThe system supports the following plugin interfaces:\\n\\n1. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for translating between Kafka Connect's runtime data format and byte[]. Supports ServiceLoader discovery and metrics registration.\\n\\n2. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Similar to Converter but specifically for processing message headers.\\n\\n3. **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that write data from Kafka to external systems.\\n\\n4. **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that read data from external systems into Kafka.\\n\\n5. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base abstract class for both source and sink connectors defining the common interface.\\n\\n### Dependency Injection via Plugins Class\\n\\nThe **Plugins** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) serves as the central dependency injection container that:\\n\\n1. **Initialization**: Constructor accepts configuration properties, discovers plugin locations, creates DelegatingClassLoader, and scans for plugins using both ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner based on PluginDiscoveryMode.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Discovery Flow**: initLoaders() method orchestrates the scanning process:\\n   - Calls ServiceLoaderScanner.discoverPlugins() for SERVICE_LOAD mode\\n   - Calls ReflectionScanner.discoverPlugins() for ONLY_SCAN mode\\n   - Merges results and installs them in DelegatingClassLoader\\n   - Reports compatibility issues if plugins lack ServiceLoader manifests\\n\\n3. **Plugin Instantiation**: Provides methods like newConverter(), newHeaderConverter(), newConnector() that:\\n   - Load the plugin class using the appropriate ClassLoader\\n   - Swap the thread context ClassLoader to the plugin's ClassLoader\\n   - Instantiate the plugin using Utils.newInstance()\\n   - Configure the plugin if it implements Configurable\\n\\n4. **ClassLoader Swapping**: Uses LoaderSwap (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) to safely swap the thread context ClassLoader during plugin instantiation and initialization.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Querying**: Provides accessor methods for different plugin types (converters(), headerConverters(), sinkConnectors(), sourceConnectors(), etc.) that query PluginScanResult.\\n\\n### Utility Functions\\n\\n**PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) provides utility methods for:\\n- Determining plugin locations from configuration\\n- Creating plugin sources (classpath and isolated)\\n- Checking if classes should be loaded in isolation\\n- Computing plugin aliases for shorthand reference\\n- Managing plugin version requirements\\n\\n### Configuration and Recommendations\\n\\n**PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java) provides ConfigDef Recommender implementations for plugin configuration fields, enabling dynamic discovery and recommendation of available plugins.\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe plugin system uses ClassLoader isolation combined with reflection-based and ServiceLoader-based discovery to provide flexible, extensible plugin architecture. The Plugins class acts as a service locator/dependency injector, managing plugin lifecycle including discovery, instantiation, and dependency injection through a type-safe interface-based architecture. The LoaderSwap pattern ensures proper ClassLoader management throughout the plugin lifecycle, enabling plugins with different dependencies to coexist without conflicts.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":11064,"cache_read_input_tokens":89422,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":11064},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b8b28337-3ba2-49a0-ba93-d3ebabba97a3","uuid":"381e012f-eed7-4457-a041-b2b4231a3288"}

classloading. The system is located in the 'sg-evals/kafka--0753c489' repository under the connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ package.\\n\\n## Core Architecture\\n\\n### ClassLoader Hierarchy\\nThe system uses a custom classloader hierarchy to provide plugin isolation:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that extends URLClassLoader and implements child-first delegation for loading isolated plugins. Each plugin location gets its own PluginClassLoader instance.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A URLClassLoader that delegates class loading to multiple PluginClassLoader instances based on the requested class. It maintains a registry of discovered plugins and routes class loading requests to the appropriate PluginClassLoader.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory class that creates both DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances with support for security manager compatibility.\\n\\n### Plugin Discovery Mechanism\\n\\nThe plugin scanning system uses reflection and Java ServiceLoader to discover plugins:\\n\\n1. **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java): Abstract base class defining the plugin scanning interface with methods to discover plugins from plugin sources.\\n\\n2. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Classgraph library to perform reflection-based discovery. It scans for concrete implementations of plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy) and collects version information via plugin reflection.\\n\\n3. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins registered in META-INF/services/ configuration files.\\n\\n4. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A Java record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, multi-JAR directory, or class hierarchy), including the ClassLoader and URLs to scan.\\n\\n### Plugin Metadata and Description\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc<T>** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): Generic descriptor class that holds metadata for a discovered plugin including the plugin class, version, type, and associated ClassLoader. Implements Comparable for sorting plugins by version and location.\\n\\n2. **PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java): Enumeration of plugin interface types: SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_POLICY.\\n\\n3. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Container for scan results holding sorted sets of PluginDesc instances for each plugin type, with support for merging multiple scan results.\\n\\n### Interface-Based Plugin Types\\n\\nThe system supports the following plugin interfaces:\\n\\n1. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for translating between Kafka Connect's runtime data format and byte[]. Supports ServiceLoader discovery and metrics registration.\\n\\n2. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Similar to Converter but specifically for processing message headers.\\n\\n3. **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that write data from Kafka to external systems.\\n\\n4. **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that read data from external systems into Kafka.\\n\\n5. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base abstract class for both source and sink connectors defining the common interface.\\n\\n### Dependency Injection via Plugins Class\\n\\nThe **Plugins** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) serves as the central dependency injection container that:\\n\\n1. **Initialization**: Constructor accepts configuration properties, discovers plugin locations, creates DelegatingClassLoader, and scans for plugins using both ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner based on PluginDiscoveryMode.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Discovery Flow**: initLoaders() method orchestrates the scanning process:\\n   - Calls ServiceLoaderScanner.discoverPlugins() for SERVICE_LOAD mode\\n   - Calls ReflectionScanner.discoverPlugins() for ONLY_SCAN mode\\n   - Merges results and installs them in DelegatingClassLoader\\n   - Reports compatibility issues if plugins lack ServiceLoader manifests\\n\\n3. **Plugin Instantiation**: Provides methods like newConverter(), newHeaderConverter(), newConnector() that:\\n   - Load the plugin class using the appropriate ClassLoader\\n   - Swap the thread context ClassLoader to the plugin's ClassLoader\\n   - Instantiate the plugin using Utils.newInstance()\\n   - Configure the plugin if it implements Configurable\\n\\n4. **ClassLoader Swapping**: Uses LoaderSwap (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) to safely swap the thread context ClassLoader during plugin instantiation and initialization.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Querying**: Provides accessor methods for different plugin types (converters(), headerConverters(), sinkConnectors(), sourceConnectors(), etc.) that query PluginScanResult.\\n\\n### Utility Functions\\n\\n**PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) provides utility methods for:\\n- Determining plugin locations from configuration\\n- Creating plugin sources (classpath and isolated)\\n- Checking if classes should be loaded in isolation\\n- Computing plugin aliases for shorthand reference\\n- Managing plugin version requirements\\n\\n### Configuration and Recommendations\\n\\n**PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java) provides ConfigDef Recommender implementations for plugin configuration fields, enabling dynamic discovery and recommendation of available plugins.\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe plugin system uses ClassLoader isolation combined with reflection-based and ServiceLoader-based discovery to provide flexible, extensible plugin architecture. The Plugins class acts as a service locator/dependency injector, managing plugin lifecycle including discovery, instantiation, and dependency injection through a type-safe interface-based architecture. The LoaderSwap pattern ensures proper ClassLoader management throughout the plugin lifecycle, enabling plugins with different dependencies to coexist without conflicts.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
